\doxysection{QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular Class Reference}
\hypertarget{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular}{}\label{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular}\index{QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}}


The main container for polar plots, representing the angular axis as a circle.  




{\ttfamily \#include $<$qcustomplot.\+h$>$}

\end{DoxyCompactItemize}


\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
The main container for polar plots, representing the angular axis as a circle. 

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
In this \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot}{QCustom\+Plot} version, polar plots are a tech preview. Expect documentation and functionality to be incomplete, as well as changing public interfaces in the future. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a0afb3e5773529e4bd20e448f81be4d2a_a0afb3e5773529e4bd20e448f81be4d2a}\index{QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}!SizeConstraintRect@{SizeConstraintRect}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SizeConstraintRect}{SizeConstraintRect}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a0afb3e5773529e4bd20e448f81be4d2a_a0afb3e5773529e4bd20e448f81be4d2a} 
enum \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a0afb3e5773529e4bd20e448f81be4d2a_a0afb3e5773529e4bd20e448f81be4d2a}{QCPLayout\+Element\+::\+Size\+Constraint\+Rect}}\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Defines to which rect of a layout element the size constraints that can be set via \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b}{set\+Minimum\+Size} and \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a74eb5280a737ab44833d506db65efd95_a74eb5280a737ab44833d506db65efd95}{set\+Maximum\+Size} apply. The outer rect (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c}{outer\+Rect}) includes the margins (e.\+g. in the case of a \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect}{QCPAxis\+Rect} the axis labels), whereas the inner rect (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4}{rect}) does not.

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a0d83360e05735735aaf6d7983c56374d_a0d83360e05735735aaf6d7983c56374d}\index{QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}!UpdatePhase@{UpdatePhase}}
\index{UpdatePhase@{UpdatePhase}!QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{UpdatePhase}{UpdatePhase}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a0d83360e05735735aaf6d7983c56374d_a0d83360e05735735aaf6d7983c56374d} 
enum \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a0d83360e05735735aaf6d7983c56374d_a0d83360e05735735aaf6d7983c56374d}{QCPLayout\+Element\+::\+Update\+Phase}}\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Defines the phases of the update process, that happens just before a replot. At each phase, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a9f2dfb377cdf3ce22a451fa9d3ab47e6_a9f2dfb377cdf3ce22a451fa9d3ab47e6}{update} is called with the according Update\+Phase value. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}[2]{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{upPreparation@{upPreparation}!QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}}\index{QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}!upPreparation@{upPreparation}}}\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a0d83360e05735735aaf6d7983c56374d_a0d83360e05735735aaf6d7983c56374dad6119882eba136357c2f627992e527d3}\label{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a0d83360e05735735aaf6d7983c56374d_a0d83360e05735735aaf6d7983c56374d} 
up\+Preparation&Phase used for any type of preparation that needs to be done before margin calculation and layout. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{upMargins@{upMargins}!QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}}\index{QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}!upMargins@{upMargins}}}\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a0d83360e05735735aaf6d7983c56374d_a0d83360e05735735aaf6d7983c56374da288cb59a92280e47261a341f2813e676}\label{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a0d83360e05735735aaf6d7983c56374d_a0d83360e05735735aaf6d7983c56374d} 
up\+Margins&Phase in which the margins are calculated and set. \\

\doxysubsection{Member Function Documentation}
\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_ac5333ac2429f6d6223c5890ab32fda38_ac5333ac2429f6d6223c5890ab32fda38}\index{QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}!addRadialAxis@{addRadialAxis}}
\index{addRadialAxis@{addRadialAxis}!QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{addRadialAxis()}{addRadialAxis()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_ac5333ac2429f6d6223c5890ab32fda38_ac5333ac2429f6d6223c5890ab32fda38} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_radial}{QCPPolar\+Axis\+Radial}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular\+::add\+Radial\+Axis (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_radial}{QCPPolar\+Axis\+Radial}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{axis}{ = {\ttfamily 0}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Adds a new axis to the axis rect side specified with {\itshape type}, and returns it. If {\itshape axis} is 0, a new \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis}{QCPAxis} instance is created internally. \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot}{QCustom\+Plot} owns the returned axis, so if you want to remove an axis, use remove\+Axis instead of deleting it manually.

You may inject \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis}{QCPAxis} instances (or subclasses of \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis}{QCPAxis}) by setting {\itshape axis} to an axis that was previously created outside \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot}{QCustom\+Plot}. It is important to note that \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot}{QCustom\+Plot} takes ownership of the axis, so you may not delete it afterwards. Further, the {\itshape axis} must have been created with this axis rect as parent and with the same axis type as specified in {\itshape type}. If this is not the case, a debug output is generated, the axis is not added, and the method returns 0.

This method can not be used to move {\itshape axis} between axis rects. The same {\itshape axis} instance must not be added multiple times to the same or different axis rects.

If an axis rect side already contains one or more axes, the lower and upper endings of the new axis (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_a08af1c72db9ae4dc8cb8a973d44405ab_a08af1c72db9ae4dc8cb8a973d44405ab}{QCPAxis\+::set\+Lower\+Ending}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_a69119b892fc306f651763596685aa377_a69119b892fc306f651763596685aa377}{QCPAxis\+::set\+Upper\+Ending}) are set to \doxylink{class_q_c_p_line_ending_a5ef16e6876b4b74959c7261d8d4c2cd5_a5ef16e6876b4b74959c7261d8d4c2cd5a126c390f0c359fcd8df1fc5e38d26d5b}{QCPLine\+Ending\+::es\+Half\+Bar}.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
add\+Axes, setup\+Full\+Axes\+Box 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

Returns the pixel position of the bottom border of this axis rect. Margins are not taken into account here, so the returned value is with respect to the inner \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4}{rect}. \Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a7342e0dd62b71f81b993c38db6fa4d5b_a7342e0dd62b71f81b993c38db6fa4d5b}\index{QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}!bottomLeft@{bottomLeft}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a95fa9af1bcb033be5c394ec2767b000e_a95fa9af1bcb033be5c394ec2767b000e} 
QList$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_layout_element}{QCPLayout\+Element}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} $>$ QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular\+::elements (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{recursive}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Returns a list of all child elements in this layout element. If {\itshape recursive} is true, all sub-\/child elements are included in the list, too.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
There may be {\ttfamily nullptr} entries in the returned list. For example, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid}{QCPLayout\+Grid} may have empty cells which yield {\ttfamily nullptr} at the respective index. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a7368a360c385cf4e3cb63e8a40795bab_a7368a360c385cf4e3cb63e8a40795bab}\index{QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}!getPartAt@{getPartAt}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{getPartAt()}{getPartAt()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a7368a360c385cf4e3cb63e8a40795bab_a7368a360c385cf4e3cb63e8a40795bab} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a342afffd77fa1e8b30778b29a26eb416_a342afffd77fa1e8b30778b29a26eb416}{QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular\+::\+Selectable\+Part}} QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular\+::get\+Part\+At (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const QPointF \&}]{pos}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}

Returns the part of the axis that is hit by {\itshape pos} (in pixels). The return value of this function is independent of the user-\/selectable parts defined with \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_af475366740d070e622e291dd30e26026_af475366740d070e622e291dd30e26026}{set\+Selectable\+Parts}. Further, this function does not change the current selection state of the axis.

If the axis is not visible (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_a3bed99ddc396b48ce3ebfdc0418744f8_a3bed99ddc396b48ce3ebfdc0418744f8}{set\+Visible}), this function always returns \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a342afffd77fa1e8b30778b29a26eb416_a342afffd77fa1e8b30778b29a26eb416a4cde0e8357b4ed68dd516694a347b232}{sp\+None}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_element_ad96efb977a26e360e8a64a4c1e56456d_ad96efb977a26e360e8a64a4c1e56456d} 
QSize QCPLayout\+Element\+::maximum\+Outer\+Size\+Hint (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}, {\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Returns the suggested maximum size this layout element (the \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c}{outer\+Rect}) may be expanded to, if no manual maximum size is set.

if a maximum size (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a74eb5280a737ab44833d506db65efd95_a74eb5280a737ab44833d506db65efd95}{set\+Maximum\+Size}) was not set manually, parent layouts use the returned size (usually indirectly through \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_add49fd6843821a6126914b837ed52e22_add49fd6843821a6126914b837ed52e22}{QCPLayout\+::get\+Final\+Maximum\+Outer\+Size}) to determine the maximum allowed size of this layout element.

A manual maximum size is considered set if it is smaller than Qt\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily QWIDGETSIZE\+\_\+\+MAX}.

The default implementation simply returns {\ttfamily QWIDGETSIZE\+\_\+\+MAX} for both width and height, implying no suggested maximum size. Reimplementations may use their detailed knowledge about the layout element\textquotesingle{}s content to provide size hints. 

Reimplemented in \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a41ce0014c220d77b909e2ca937f0e599_a41ce0014c220d77b909e2ca937f0e599}{QCPLayout\+Grid}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_text_element_ae82475b50c10a5b3314d996d50ae536b_ae82475b50c10a5b3314d996d50ae536b}{QCPText\+Element}}.

\end{center}

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a46789036c4fcb190fa374f91321d7c09_a46789036c4fcb190fa374f91321d7c09}\index{QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}!minimumOuterSizeHint@{minimumOuterSizeHint}}
\index{minimumOuterSizeHint@{minimumOuterSizeHint}!QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{minimumOuterSizeHint()}{minimumOuterSizeHint()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a46789036c4fcb190fa374f91321d7c09_a46789036c4fcb190fa374f91321d7c09} 
QSize QCPLayout\+Element\+::minimum\+Outer\+Size\+Hint (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}, {\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Returns the suggested minimum size this layout element (the \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c}{outer\+Rect}) may be compressed to, if no manual minimum size is set.

if a minimum size (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b}{set\+Minimum\+Size}) was not set manually, parent layouts use the returned size (usually indirectly through \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_a864fddc84721f186663faf3683f1fa70_a864fddc84721f186663faf3683f1fa70}{QCPLayout\+::get\+Final\+Minimum\+Outer\+Size}) to determine the minimum allowed size of this layout element.

A manual minimum size is considered set if it is non-\/zero.

The default implementation simply returns the sum of the horizontal margins for the width and the sum of the vertical margins for the height. Reimplementations may use their detailed knowledge about the layout element\textquotesingle{}s content to provide size hints. 

Reimplemented in \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a0438bc58b4d3894d01db95b08d4268df_a0438bc58b4d3894d01db95b08d4268df}{QCPLayout\+Grid}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_plottable_legend_item_a8b543f3ac32b2fe59326e01c1101b3b8_a8b543f3ac32b2fe59326e01c1101b3b8}{QCPPlottable\+Legend\+Item}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_polar_legend_item_a17e2c0da8308a014b1d4339131215217_a17e2c0da8308a014b1d4339131215217}{QCPPolar\+Legend\+Item}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_text_element_a47b8541f55ff520c557e0f27461f109e_a47b8541f55ff520c557e0f27461f109e}{QCPText\+Element}}.

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layerable_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81}\index{QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}!mouseDoubleClickEvent@{mouseDoubleClickEvent}}
\index{mouseDoubleClickEvent@{mouseDoubleClickEvent}!QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mouseDoubleClickEvent()}{mouseDoubleClickEvent()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layerable_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81} 
void QCPLayerable\+::mouse\+Double\+Click\+Event (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{QMouse\+Event \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{event}{, }\item[{const QVariant \&}]{details}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}, {\ttfamily [inherited]}}

This event gets called when the user presses the mouse button a second time in a double-\/click, while the cursor is over the layerable. Whether a cursor is over the layerable is decided by a preceding call to \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_abb390ae7656b7241acfe4ed9ea56f1ae_abb390ae7656b7241acfe4ed9ea56f1ae}{select\+Test}.

The \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81}{mouse\+Double\+Click\+Event} is called instead of the second \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a58b246497deae08694cfb40e0b4273eb_a58b246497deae08694cfb40e0b4273eb}{mouse\+Press\+Event}. So in the case of a double-\/click, the event succession is {\itshape press\+Event -- release\+Event -- double\+Click\+Event -- release\+Event}.

The current pixel position of the cursor on the \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot}{QCustom\+Plot} widget is accessible via {\ttfamily event-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}pos()}. The parameter {\itshape details} contains layerable-\/specific details about the hit, which were generated in the previous call to \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_abb390ae7656b7241acfe4ed9ea56f1ae_abb390ae7656b7241acfe4ed9ea56f1ae}{select\+Test}. For example, One-\/dimensional plottables like \doxylink{class_q_c_p_graph}{QCPGraph} or \doxylink{class_q_c_p_bars}{QCPBars} convey the clicked data point in the {\itshape details} parameter, as \doxylink{class_q_c_p_data_selection}{QCPData\+Selection} packed as QVariant. Multi-\/part objects convey the specific {\ttfamily Selectable\+Part} that was hit (e.\+g. \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_abee4c7a54c468b1385dfce2c898b115f_abee4c7a54c468b1385dfce2c898b115f}{QCPAxis\+::\+Selectable\+Part} in the case of axes).

Similarly to \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a58b246497deae08694cfb40e0b4273eb_a58b246497deae08694cfb40e0b4273eb}{mouse\+Press\+Event}, once a layerable has accepted the \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81}{mouse\+Double\+Click\+Event}, it is considered the mouse grabber and will receive all following calls to \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a5e2b49c56b57abc2ac2005e330ef1ee7_a5e2b49c56b57abc2ac2005e330ef1ee7}{mouse\+Move\+Event} and \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_af1514482693091c40fbe802fce3c1db4_af1514482693091c40fbe802fce3c1db4}{mouse\+Release\+Event} for this mouse interaction (a "{}mouse interaction"{} in this context ends with the release).

The default implementation does nothing except explicitly ignoring the event with {\ttfamily event-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}ignore()}.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a58b246497deae08694cfb40e0b4273eb_a58b246497deae08694cfb40e0b4273eb}{mouse\+Press\+Event}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a5e2b49c56b57abc2ac2005e330ef1ee7_a5e2b49c56b57abc2ac2005e330ef1ee7}{mouse\+Move\+Event}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_af1514482693091c40fbe802fce3c1db4_af1514482693091c40fbe802fce3c1db4}{mouse\+Release\+Event}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a78f5d8c2c942fa1c47dcef5d96616e8d_a78f5d8c2c942fa1c47dcef5d96616e8d}{wheel\+Event} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}


Reimplemented in \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_text_element_a2272ff775ab385f612e9fd39773de7c0_a2272ff775ab385f612e9fd39773de7c0}{QCPText\+Element}}.

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a5e2b49c56b57abc2ac2005e330ef1ee7_a5e2b49c56b57abc2ac2005e330ef1ee7}\index{QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}!mouseMoveEvent@{mouseMoveEvent}}
\index{mouseMoveEvent@{mouseMoveEvent}!QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mouseMoveEvent()}{mouseMoveEvent()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a5e2b49c56b57abc2ac2005e330ef1ee7_a5e2b49c56b57abc2ac2005e330ef1ee7} 
void QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular\+::mouse\+Move\+Event (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{QMouse\+Event \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{event}{, }\item[{const QPointF \&}]{start\+Pos}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}

This event gets called when the user moves the mouse while holding a mouse button, after this layerable has become the mouse grabber by accepting the preceding \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a58b246497deae08694cfb40e0b4273eb_a58b246497deae08694cfb40e0b4273eb}{mouse\+Press\+Event}.

The current pixel position of the cursor on the \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot}{QCustom\+Plot} widget is accessible via {\ttfamily event-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}pos()}. The parameter {\itshape start\+Pos} indicates the position where the initial \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a58b246497deae08694cfb40e0b4273eb_a58b246497deae08694cfb40e0b4273eb}{mouse\+Press\+Event} occurred, that started the mouse interaction.

The default implementation does nothing.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a58b246497deae08694cfb40e0b4273eb_a58b246497deae08694cfb40e0b4273eb}{mouse\+Press\+Event}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_af1514482693091c40fbe802fce3c1db4_af1514482693091c40fbe802fce3c1db4}{mouse\+Release\+Event}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81}{mouse\+Double\+Click\+Event}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a78f5d8c2c942fa1c47dcef5d96616e8d_a78f5d8c2c942fa1c47dcef5d96616e8d}{wheel\+Event}

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a58b246497deae08694cfb40e0b4273eb_a58b246497deae08694cfb40e0b4273eb}\index{QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}!mousePressEvent@{mousePressEvent}}
\index{mousePressEvent@{mousePressEvent}!QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mousePressEvent()}{mousePressEvent()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a58b246497deae08694cfb40e0b4273eb_a58b246497deae08694cfb40e0b4273eb} 
void QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular\+::mouse\+Press\+Event (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{QMouse\+Event \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{event}{, }\item[{const QVariant \&}]{details}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}

This event gets called when the user presses a mouse button while the cursor is over the layerable. Whether a cursor is over the layerable is decided by a preceding call to \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_abb390ae7656b7241acfe4ed9ea56f1ae_abb390ae7656b7241acfe4ed9ea56f1ae}{select\+Test}.

The current pixel position of the cursor on the \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot}{QCustom\+Plot} widget is accessible via {\ttfamily event-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}pos()}. The parameter {\itshape details} contains layerable-\/specific details about the hit, which were generated in the previous call to \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_abb390ae7656b7241acfe4ed9ea56f1ae_abb390ae7656b7241acfe4ed9ea56f1ae}{select\+Test}. For example, One-\/dimensional plottables like \doxylink{class_q_c_p_graph}{QCPGraph} or \doxylink{class_q_c_p_bars}{QCPBars} convey the clicked data point in the {\itshape details} parameter, as \doxylink{class_q_c_p_data_selection}{QCPData\+Selection} packed as QVariant. Multi-\/part objects convey the specific {\ttfamily Selectable\+Part} that was hit (e.\+g. \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_abee4c7a54c468b1385dfce2c898b115f_abee4c7a54c468b1385dfce2c898b115f}{QCPAxis\+::\+Selectable\+Part} in the case of axes).

\doxylink{class_q_custom_plot}{QCustom\+Plot} uses an event propagation system that works the same as Qt\textquotesingle{}s system. If your layerable doesn\textquotesingle{}t reimplement the \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a58b246497deae08694cfb40e0b4273eb_a58b246497deae08694cfb40e0b4273eb}{mouse\+Press\+Event} or explicitly calls {\ttfamily event-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}ignore()} in its reimplementation, the event will be propagated to the next layerable in the stacking order.

Once a layerable has accepted the \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a58b246497deae08694cfb40e0b4273eb_a58b246497deae08694cfb40e0b4273eb}{mouse\+Press\+Event}, it is considered the mouse grabber and will receive all following calls to \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a5e2b49c56b57abc2ac2005e330ef1ee7_a5e2b49c56b57abc2ac2005e330ef1ee7}{mouse\+Move\+Event} or \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_af1514482693091c40fbe802fce3c1db4_af1514482693091c40fbe802fce3c1db4}{mouse\+Release\+Event} for this mouse interaction (a "{}mouse interaction"{} in this context ends with the release).

The default implementation does nothing except explicitly ignoring the event with {\ttfamily event-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}ignore()}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_af5d19f1b60eba481e735829c5e9ec433_af5d19f1b60eba481e735829c5e9ec433} 
void QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular\+::move\+Range (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{double}]{diff}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

If the scale type (set\+Scale\+Type) is st\+Linear, {\itshape diff} is added to the lower and upper bounds of the range. The range is simply moved by {\itshape diff}.

If the scale type is st\+Logarithmic, the range bounds are multiplied by {\itshape diff}. This corresponds to an apparent "{}linear"{} move in logarithmic scaling by a distance of log(diff). Here is the call graph for this function\+:\nopagebreak

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c} 
QRect QCPLayout\+Element\+::outer\+Rect (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Returns the outer rect of this layout element. The outer rect is the inner rect expanded by the margins (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a8f450b1f3f992ad576fce2c63d8b79cf_a8f450b1f3f992ad576fce2c63d8b79cf}{set\+Margins}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d}{set\+Auto\+Margins}). The outer rect is used (and set via \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a38975ea13e36de8e53391ce41d94bc0f_a38975ea13e36de8e53391ce41d94bc0f}{set\+Outer\+Rect}) by the parent \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout}{QCPLayout} to control the size of this layout element.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4}{rect} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\index{parentLayerable@{parentLayerable}!QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{parentLayerable()}{parentLayerable()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layerable_aa78b7e644d2c519e1a9a6f2ac5fcd858_aa78b7e644d2c519e1a9a6f2ac5fcd858} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_layerable}{QCPLayerable}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} QCPLayerable\+::parent\+Layerable (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Returns the parent layerable of this layerable. The parent layerable is used to provide visibility hierarchies in conjunction with the method \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_ab054e88f15d485defcb95e7376f119e7_ab054e88f15d485defcb95e7376f119e7}{real\+Visibility}. This way, layerables only get drawn if their parent layerables are visible, too.

Note that a parent layerable is not necessarily also the QObject parent for memory management. Further, a layerable doesn\textquotesingle{}t always have a parent layerable, so this function may return {\ttfamily nullptr}.

A parent layerable is set implicitly when placed inside layout elements and doesn\textquotesingle{}t need to be set manually by the user. Here is the caller graph for this function\+:\nopagebreak

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layerable_ab054e88f15d485defcb95e7376f119e7_ab054e88f15d485defcb95e7376f119e7}\index{QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}!realVisibility@{realVisibility}}
\index{realVisibility@{realVisibility}!QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{realVisibility()}{realVisibility()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layerable_ab054e88f15d485defcb95e7376f119e7_ab054e88f15d485defcb95e7376f119e7} 
bool QCPLayerable\+::real\+Visibility (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Returns whether this layerable is visible, taking the visibility of the layerable parent and the visibility of this layerable\textquotesingle{}s layer into account. This is the method that is consulted to decide whether a layerable shall be drawn or not.

If this layerable has a direct layerable parent (usually set via hierarchies implemented in subclasses, like in the case of \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element}{QCPLayout\+Element}), this function returns true only if this layerable has its visibility set to true and the parent layerable\textquotesingle{}s \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_ab054e88f15d485defcb95e7376f119e7_ab054e88f15d485defcb95e7376f119e7}{real\+Visibility} returns true. Here is the call graph for this function\+:\nopagebreak

\begin{center}

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4}\index{QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}!rect@{rect}}
\index{rect@{rect}!QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{rect()}{rect()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4} 
QRect QCPLayout\+Element\+::rect (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Returns the inner rect of this layout element. The inner rect is the outer rect (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c}{outer\+Rect}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a38975ea13e36de8e53391ce41d94bc0f_a38975ea13e36de8e53391ce41d94bc0f}{set\+Outer\+Rect}) shrinked by the margins (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a8f450b1f3f992ad576fce2c63d8b79cf_a8f450b1f3f992ad576fce2c63d8b79cf}{set\+Margins}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d}{set\+Auto\+Margins}).

In some cases, the area between outer and inner rect is left blank. In other cases the margin area is used to display peripheral graphics while the main content is in the inner rect. This is where automatic margin calculation becomes interesting because it allows the layout element to adapt the margins to the peripheral graphics it wants to draw. For example, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect}{QCPAxis\+Rect} draws the axis labels and tick labels in the margin area, thus needs to adjust the margins (if \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d}{set\+Auto\+Margins} is enabled) according to the space required by the labels of the axes.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c}{outer\+Rect} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\end{center}
\end{figure}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{right()}{right()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_ab5d7d189cffd21294a23ece4f1cd9ca8_ab5d7d189cffd21294a23ece4f1cd9ca8} 
int QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular\+::right (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Returns the pixel position of the right border of this axis rect. Margins are not taken into account here, so the returned value is with respect to the inner \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4}{rect}. \Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_ae101a2ad79391909da0c0f1f08f9e872_ae101a2ad79391909da0c0f1f08f9e872}\index{QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}!scaleRange@{scaleRange}}
\index{scaleRange@{scaleRange}!QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{scaleRange()}{scaleRange()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_ae101a2ad79391909da0c0f1f08f9e872_ae101a2ad79391909da0c0f1f08f9e872} 
void QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular\+::scale\+Range (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{double}]{factor}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Scales the range of this axis by {\itshape factor} around the center of the current axis range. For example, if {\itshape factor} is 2.\+0, then the axis range will double its size, and the point at the axis range center won\textquotesingle{}t have changed its position in the \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot}{QCustom\+Plot} widget (i.\+e. coordinates around the center will have moved symmetrically closer).

If you wish to scale around a different coordinate than the current axis range center, use the overload \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a3f1783650404238080da4d5fd99dd81e_a3f1783650404238080da4d5fd99dd81e}{scale\+Range(double factor, double center)}. \end{center}
\end{figure}

\end{center}
\end{figure}
\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a3f1783650404238080da4d5fd99dd81e_a3f1783650404238080da4d5fd99dd81e}\index{QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}!scaleRange@{scaleRange}}
\index{scaleRange@{scaleRange}!QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{scaleRange()}{scaleRange()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a3f1783650404238080da4d5fd99dd81e_a3f1783650404238080da4d5fd99dd81e} 
void QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular\+::scale\+Range (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{double}]{factor}{, }\item[{double}]{center}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

This is an overloaded member function, provided for convenience. It differs from the above function only in what argument(s) it accepts.

Scales the range of this axis by {\itshape factor} around the coordinate {\itshape center}. For example, if {\itshape factor} is 2.\+0, {\itshape center} is 1.\+0, then the axis range will double its size, and the point at coordinate 1.\+0 won\textquotesingle{}t have changed its position in the \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot}{QCustom\+Plot} widget (i.\+e. coordinates around 1.\+0 will have moved symmetrically closer to 1.\+0).

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_abb390ae7656b7241acfe4ed9ea56f1ae_abb390ae7656b7241acfe4ed9ea56f1ae}\index{QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}!selectTest@{selectTest}}
\index{selectTest@{selectTest}!QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{selectTest()}{selectTest()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_abb390ae7656b7241acfe4ed9ea56f1ae_abb390ae7656b7241acfe4ed9ea56f1ae} 
double QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular\+::select\+Test (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const QPointF \&}]{pos}{, }\item[{bool}]{only\+Selectable}{, }\item[{QVariant \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{details}{ = {\ttfamily 0}}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Layout elements are sensitive to events inside their outer rect. If {\itshape pos} is within the outer rect, this method returns a value corresponding to 0.\+99 times the parent plot\textquotesingle{}s selection tolerance. However, layout elements are not selectable by default. So if {\itshape only\+Selectable} is true, -\/1.\+0 is returned.

See \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_a272989087fc8c4357b4ba614f9922336_a272989087fc8c4357b4ba614f9922336}{QCPLayerable\+::select\+Test} for a general explanation of this virtual method.

\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element}{QCPLayout\+Element} subclasses may reimplement this method to provide more specific selection test behaviour. 

Reimplemented from \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a62d60f1b0ee9bb23e38811d71586d79c_a62d60f1b0ee9bb23e38811d71586d79c}{QCPLayout\+Element}}.

\end{center}
\end{figure}

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layout_element_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d}\index{QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}!setAutoMargins@{setAutoMargins}}
\index{setAutoMargins@{setAutoMargins}!QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setAutoMargins()}{setAutoMargins()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_element_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d} 
void QCPLayout\+Element\+::set\+Auto\+Margins (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{QCP\+::\+Margin\+Sides}]{sides}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Sets on which sides the margin shall be calculated automatically. If a side is calculated automatically, a minimum margin value may be provided with \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a0a8a17abc16b7923159fcc7608f94673_a0a8a17abc16b7923159fcc7608f94673}{set\+Minimum\+Margins}. If a side is set to be controlled manually, the value may be specified with \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a8f450b1f3f992ad576fce2c63d8b79cf_a8f450b1f3f992ad576fce2c63d8b79cf}{set\+Margins}.

Margin sides that are under automatic control may participate in a \doxylink{class_q_c_p_margin_group}{QCPMargin\+Group} (see \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a516e56f76b6bc100e8e71d329866847d_a516e56f76b6bc100e8e71d329866847d}{set\+Margin\+Group}), to synchronize (align) it with other layout elements in the plot.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a0a8a17abc16b7923159fcc7608f94673_a0a8a17abc16b7923159fcc7608f94673}{set\+Minimum\+Margins}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a8f450b1f3f992ad576fce2c63d8b79cf_a8f450b1f3f992ad576fce2c63d8b79cf}{set\+Margins}, \doxylink{namespace_q_c_p_a7e487e3e2ccb62ab7771065bab7cae54_a7e487e3e2ccb62ab7771065bab7cae54}{QCP\+::\+Margin\+Side} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a7c0dd85939536498818b49a89c1e2433_a7c0dd85939536498818b49a89c1e2433}\index{QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}!setBackground@{setBackground}}
\index{setBackground@{setBackground}!QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setBackground()}{setBackground()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a7c0dd85939536498818b49a89c1e2433_a7c0dd85939536498818b49a89c1e2433} 
void QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular\+::set\+Background (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const QBrush \&}]{brush}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

This is an overloaded member function, provided for convenience. It differs from the above function only in what argument(s) it accepts.

Sets {\itshape brush} as the background brush. The axis rect background will be filled with this brush. Since axis rects place themselves on the "{}background"{} layer by default, the axis rect backgrounds are usually drawn below everything else.

The brush will be drawn before (under) any background pixmap, which may be specified with \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a11e1e23ea1d52abded4b7fab42c10e60_a11e1e23ea1d52abded4b7fab42c10e60}{set\+Background(const QPixmap \&pm)}.

To disable drawing of a background brush, set {\itshape brush} to Qt\+::\+No\+Brush.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a11e1e23ea1d52abded4b7fab42c10e60_a11e1e23ea1d52abded4b7fab42c10e60}{set\+Background(const QPixmap \&pm)} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a11e1e23ea1d52abded4b7fab42c10e60_a11e1e23ea1d52abded4b7fab42c10e60}\index{QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}!setBackground@{setBackground}}
\index{setBackground@{setBackground}!QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setBackground()}{setBackground()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a11e1e23ea1d52abded4b7fab42c10e60_a11e1e23ea1d52abded4b7fab42c10e60} 
void QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular\+::set\+Background (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const QPixmap \&}]{pm}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets {\itshape pm} as the axis background pixmap. The axis background pixmap will be drawn inside the axis rect. Since axis rects place themselves on the "{}background"{} layer by default, the axis rect backgrounds are usually drawn below everything else.

For cases where the provided pixmap doesn\textquotesingle{}t have the same size as the axis rect, scaling can be enabled with \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_af2a38b983f2ebe8fe10ca256b119a90c_af2a38b983f2ebe8fe10ca256b119a90c}{set\+Background\+Scaled} and the scaling mode (i.\+e. whether and how the aspect ratio is preserved) can be set with \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a57b0e1c12826f67cf6ce347628abcbd8_a57b0e1c12826f67cf6ce347628abcbd8}{set\+Background\+Scaled\+Mode}. To set all these options in one call, consider using the overloaded version of this function.

Below the pixmap, the axis rect may be optionally filled with a brush, if specified with \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a7c0dd85939536498818b49a89c1e2433_a7c0dd85939536498818b49a89c1e2433}{set\+Background(const QBrush \&brush)}.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_af2a38b983f2ebe8fe10ca256b119a90c_af2a38b983f2ebe8fe10ca256b119a90c}{set\+Background\+Scaled}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a57b0e1c12826f67cf6ce347628abcbd8_a57b0e1c12826f67cf6ce347628abcbd8}{set\+Background\+Scaled\+Mode}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a7c0dd85939536498818b49a89c1e2433_a7c0dd85939536498818b49a89c1e2433}{set\+Background(const QBrush \&brush)} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_af456d4aaf5f71807d88d1b8919f79355_af456d4aaf5f71807d88d1b8919f79355}\index{QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}!setBackground@{setBackground}}
\index{setBackground@{setBackground}!QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}}

void QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular\+::set\+Background (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const QPixmap \&}]{pm}{, }\item[{bool}]{scaled}{, }\item[{Qt\+::\+Aspect\+Ratio\+Mode}]{mode}{ = {\ttfamily Qt\+:\+:KeepAspectRatioByExpanding}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

This is an overloaded member function, provided for convenience. It differs from the above function only in what argument(s) it accepts.

Allows setting the background pixmap of the axis rect, whether it shall be scaled and how it shall be scaled in one call.

\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_af2a38b983f2ebe8fe10ca256b119a90c_af2a38b983f2ebe8fe10ca256b119a90c}\index{QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}!setBackgroundScaled@{setBackgroundScaled}}
\index{setBackgroundScaled@{setBackgroundScaled}!QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setBackgroundScaled()}{setBackgroundScaled()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_af2a38b983f2ebe8fe10ca256b119a90c_af2a38b983f2ebe8fe10ca256b119a90c} 
void QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular\+::set\+Background\+Scaled (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{scaled}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets whether the axis background pixmap shall be scaled to fit the axis rect or not. If {\itshape scaled} is set to true, you may control whether and how the aspect ratio of the original pixmap is preserved with \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a57b0e1c12826f67cf6ce347628abcbd8_a57b0e1c12826f67cf6ce347628abcbd8}{set\+Background\+Scaled\+Mode}.

Note that the scaled version of the original pixmap is buffered, so there is no performance penalty on replots. (Except when the axis rect dimensions are changed continuously.)

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a11e1e23ea1d52abded4b7fab42c10e60_a11e1e23ea1d52abded4b7fab42c10e60}{set\+Background}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a57b0e1c12826f67cf6ce347628abcbd8_a57b0e1c12826f67cf6ce347628abcbd8}{set\+Background\+Scaled\+Mode} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a57b0e1c12826f67cf6ce347628abcbd8_a57b0e1c12826f67cf6ce347628abcbd8}\index{QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}!setBackgroundScaledMode@{setBackgroundScaledMode}}
\index{setBackgroundScaledMode@{setBackgroundScaledMode}!QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setBackgroundScaledMode()}{setBackgroundScaledMode()}}

void QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular\+::set\+Background\+Scaled\+Mode (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Qt\+::\+Aspect\+Ratio\+Mode}]{mode}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

If scaling of the axis background pixmap is enabled (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_af2a38b983f2ebe8fe10ca256b119a90c_af2a38b983f2ebe8fe10ca256b119a90c}{set\+Background\+Scaled}), use this function to define whether and how the aspect ratio of the original pixmap passed to \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a11e1e23ea1d52abded4b7fab42c10e60_a11e1e23ea1d52abded4b7fab42c10e60}{set\+Background} is preserved. \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a11e1e23ea1d52abded4b7fab42c10e60_a11e1e23ea1d52abded4b7fab42c10e60}{set\+Background}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_af2a38b983f2ebe8fe10ca256b119a90c_af2a38b983f2ebe8fe10ca256b119a90c}{set\+Background\+Scaled} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layerable_ab0d0da6d2de45a118886d2c8e16d5a54_ab0d0da6d2de45a118886d2c8e16d5a54} 
bool QCPLayerable\+::set\+Layer (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_layer}{QCPLayer}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{layer}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Sets the {\itshape layer} of this layerable object. The object will be placed on top of the other objects already on {\itshape layer}.

If {\itshape layer} is 0, this layerable will not be on any layer and thus not appear in the plot (or interact/receive events).

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setMarginGroup()}{setMarginGroup()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a516e56f76b6bc100e8e71d329866847d_a516e56f76b6bc100e8e71d329866847d} 
void QCPLayout\+Element\+::set\+Margin\+Group (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{QCP\+::\+Margin\+Sides}]{sides}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_margin_group}{QCPMargin\+Group}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{group}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Sets the margin {\itshape group} of the specified margin {\itshape sides}.

Margin groups allow synchronizing specified margins across layout elements, see the documentation of \doxylink{class_q_c_p_margin_group}{QCPMargin\+Group}.

To unset the margin group of {\itshape sides}, set {\itshape group} to {\ttfamily nullptr}.

Note that margin groups only work for margin sides that are set to automatic (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d}{set\+Auto\+Margins}).

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setMargins()}{setMargins()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a8f450b1f3f992ad576fce2c63d8b79cf_a8f450b1f3f992ad576fce2c63d8b79cf} 
void QCPLayout\+Element\+::set\+Margins (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const QMargins \&}]{margins}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Sets the margins of this layout element. If \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d}{set\+Auto\+Margins} is disabled for some or all sides, this function is used to manually set the margin on those sides. Sides that are still set to be handled automatically are ignored and may have any value in {\itshape margins}.

The margin is the distance between the outer rect (controlled by the parent layout via \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a38975ea13e36de8e53391ce41d94bc0f_a38975ea13e36de8e53391ce41d94bc0f}{set\+Outer\+Rect}) and the inner \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4}{rect} (which usually contains the main content of this layout element).

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setMinimumSize()}{setMinimumSize()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b} 
void QCPLayout\+Element\+::set\+Minimum\+Size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const QSize \&}]{size}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Sets the minimum size of this layout element. A parent layout tries to respect the {\itshape size} here by changing row/column sizes in the layout accordingly.

If the parent layout size is not sufficient to satisfy all minimum size constraints of its child layout elements, the layout may set a size that is actually smaller than {\itshape size}. \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot}{QCustom\+Plot} propagates the layout\textquotesingle{}s size constraints to the outside by setting its own minimum QWidget size accordingly, so violations of {\itshape size} should be exceptions.

Whether this constraint applies to the inner or the outer rect can be specified with \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a361666cdcc6fbfd37344cc44be746b0f_a361666cdcc6fbfd37344cc44be746b0f}{set\+Size\+Constraint\+Rect} (see \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4}{rect} and \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c}{outer\+Rect}). \Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a3781860cc80b9a6d8be2a4f8179733dd_a3781860cc80b9a6d8be2a4f8179733dd}\index{QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}!setNumberFormat@{setNumberFormat}}
\index{setNumberFormat@{setNumberFormat}!QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setNumberFormat()}{setNumberFormat()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a3781860cc80b9a6d8be2a4f8179733dd_a3781860cc80b9a6d8be2a4f8179733dd} 
void QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular\+::set\+Number\+Format (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const QString \&}]{format\+Code}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets the number format for the numbers in tick labels. This {\itshape format\+Code} is an extended version of the format code used e.\+g. by QString\+::number() and QLocale\+::to\+String(). For reference about that, see the "{}\+Argument Formats"{} section in the detailed description of the QString class.

{\itshape format\+Code} is a string of one, two or three characters. The first character is identical to the normal format code used by Qt. In short, this means\+: \textquotesingle{}e\textquotesingle{}/\textquotesingle{}E\textquotesingle{} scientific format, \textquotesingle{}f\textquotesingle{} fixed format, \textquotesingle{}g\textquotesingle{}/\textquotesingle{}G\textquotesingle{} scientific or fixed, whichever is shorter.

The second and third characters are optional and specific to \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot}{QCustom\+Plot}\+:~\newline
 If the first char was \textquotesingle{}e\textquotesingle{} or \textquotesingle{}g\textquotesingle{}, numbers are/might be displayed in the scientific format, e.\+g. "{}5.\+5e9"{}, which might be visually unappealing in a plot. So when the second char of {\itshape format\+Code} is set to \textquotesingle{}b\textquotesingle{} (for "{}beautiful"{}), those exponential numbers are formatted in a more natural way, i.\+e. "{}5.\+5 \mbox{[}multiplication sign\mbox{]} 10 \mbox{[}superscript\mbox{]} 9"{}. By default, the multiplication sign is a centered dot. If instead a cross should be shown (as is usual in the USA), the third char of {\itshape format\+Code} can be set to \textquotesingle{}c\textquotesingle{}. The inserted multiplication signs are the UTF-\/8 characters 215 (0x\+D7) for the cross and 183 (0x\+B7) for the dot.

Examples for {\itshape format\+Code\+:} \begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily g} normal format code behaviour. If number is small, fixed format is used, if number is large, normal scientific format is used \item {\ttfamily gb} If number is small, fixed format is used, if number is large, scientific format is used with beautifully typeset decimal powers and a dot as multiplication sign \item {\ttfamily ebc} All numbers are in scientific format with beautifully typeset decimal power and a cross as multiplication sign \item {\ttfamily fb} illegal format code, since fixed format doesn\textquotesingle{}t support (or need) beautifully typeset decimal powers. Format code will be reduced to \textquotesingle{}f\textquotesingle{}. \item {\ttfamily hello} illegal format code, since first char is not \textquotesingle{}e\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}E\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}f\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}g\textquotesingle{} or \textquotesingle{}G\textquotesingle{}. Current format code will not be changed. \end{DoxyItemize}
Here is the call graph for this function\+:\nopagebreak
\begin{figure}[H]
\begin{center}

\end{center}
\end{figure}
\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a1c463fe5cbc8ddaead62b2278cfbfb35_a1c463fe5cbc8ddaead62b2278cfbfb35}\index{QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}!setNumberPrecision@{setNumberPrecision}}
\index{setNumberPrecision@{setNumberPrecision}!QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setNumberPrecision()}{setNumberPrecision()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a1c463fe5cbc8ddaead62b2278cfbfb35_a1c463fe5cbc8ddaead62b2278cfbfb35} 
void QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular\+::set\+Number\+Precision (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{precision}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets the precision of the tick label numbers. See QLocale\+::to\+String(double i, char f, int prec) for details. The effect of precisions are most notably for number Formats starting with \textquotesingle{}e\textquotesingle{}, see \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a3781860cc80b9a6d8be2a4f8179733dd_a3781860cc80b9a6d8be2a4f8179733dd}{set\+Number\+Format} \Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a38975ea13e36de8e53391ce41d94bc0f_a38975ea13e36de8e53391ce41d94bc0f}\index{QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}!setOuterRect@{setOuterRect}}
\index{setOuterRect@{setOuterRect}!QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setOuterRect()}{setOuterRect()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a38975ea13e36de8e53391ce41d94bc0f_a38975ea13e36de8e53391ce41d94bc0f} 
void QCPLayout\+Element\+::set\+Outer\+Rect (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const QRect \&}]{rect}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Sets the outer rect of this layout element. If the layout element is inside a layout, the layout sets the position and size of this layout element using this function.

Calling this function externally has no effect, since the layout will overwrite any changes to the outer rect upon the next replot.

The layout element will adapt its inner \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4}{rect} by applying the margins inward to the outer rect.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4}{rect} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

void QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular\+::set\+Range (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_range}{QCPRange}} \&}]{range}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets the range of the axis.

This slot may be connected with the \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a70f1f41494d189693e0e12f8cdd103b4_a70f1f41494d189693e0e12f8cdd103b4}{range\+Changed} signal of another axis so this axis is always synchronized with the other axis range, when it changes.

To invert the direction of an axis, use \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_adf584a9a77283842c8df20805b90b17f_adf584a9a77283842c8df20805b90b17f}{set\+Range\+Reversed}. Here is the call graph for this function\+:\nopagebreak

This is an overloaded member function, provided for convenience. It differs from the above function only in what argument(s) it accepts.

Sets the lower and upper bound of the axis range.

To invert the direction of an axis, use \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_adf584a9a77283842c8df20805b90b17f_adf584a9a77283842c8df20805b90b17f}{set\+Range\+Reversed}.

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a10d361152ed9ccf68ecf682ac82b4442_a10d361152ed9ccf68ecf682ac82b4442}\index{QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}!setRange@{setRange}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a10d361152ed9ccf68ecf682ac82b4442_a10d361152ed9ccf68ecf682ac82b4442} 
void QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular\+::set\+Range (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{double}]{position}{, }\item[{double}]{size}{, }\item[{Qt\+::\+Alignment\+Flag}]{alignment}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

This is an overloaded member function, provided for convenience. It differs from the above function only in what argument(s) it accepts.

Sets the range of the axis.

The {\itshape position} coordinate indicates together with the {\itshape alignment} parameter, where the new range will be positioned. {\itshape size} defines the size of the new axis range. {\itshape alignment} may be Qt\+::\+Align\+Left, Qt\+::\+Align\+Right or Qt\+::\+Align\+Center. This will cause the left border, right border, or center of the range to be aligned with {\itshape position}. Any other values of {\itshape alignment} will default to Qt\+::\+Align\+Center. {\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_adf584a9a77283842c8df20805b90b17f_adf584a9a77283842c8df20805b90b17f} 
void QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular\+::set\+Range\+Reversed (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{reversed}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets whether the axis range (direction) is displayed reversed. Normally, the values on horizontal axes increase left to right, on vertical axes bottom to top. When {\itshape reversed} is set to true, the direction of increasing values is inverted.

Note that the range and data interface stays the same for reversed axes, e.\+g. the {\itshape lower} part of the \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_aff1a9a85cc7f5f3493b4aae8213f7cbe_aff1a9a85cc7f5f3493b4aae8213f7cbe}{set\+Range} interface will still reference the mathematically smaller number than the {\itshape upper} part. \Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a4b395b3cd4d43caa506351d35b3f401d_a4b395b3cd4d43caa506351d35b3f401d}\index{QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}!setRangeUpper@{setRangeUpper}}
\index{setRangeUpper@{setRangeUpper}!QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setRangeUpper()}{setRangeUpper()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a4b395b3cd4d43caa506351d35b3f401d_a4b395b3cd4d43caa506351d35b3f401d} 
void QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular\+::set\+Range\+Upper (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{double}]{upper}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets the upper bound of the axis range. The lower bound is not changed. \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

void QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular\+::set\+Selectable\+Parts (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular\+::\+Selectable\+Parts \&}]{selectable\+Parts}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets whether the user can (de-\/)select the parts in {\itshape selectable} by clicking on the \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot}{QCustom\+Plot} surface. (When \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot_a5ee1e2f6ae27419deca53e75907c27e5_a5ee1e2f6ae27419deca53e75907c27e5}{QCustom\+Plot\+::set\+Interactions} contains i\+Select\+Axes.)

However, even when {\itshape selectable} is set to a value not allowing the selection of a specific part, it is still possible to set the selection of this part manually, by calling \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a42cfbfd3052682539ed239795ae1c4a8_a42cfbfd3052682539ed239795ae1c4a8}{set\+Selected\+Parts} directly.

\doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_aa033e53edcfdc5a86bc178a72606148a_aa033e53edcfdc5a86bc178a72606148a}{set\+Label\+Font}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_af475366740d070e622e291dd30e26026_af475366740d070e622e291dd30e26026}{set\+Selectable\+Parts}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a42cfbfd3052682539ed239795ae1c4a8_a42cfbfd3052682539ed239795ae1c4a8}{set\+Selected\+Parts}, \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot_a5ee1e2f6ae27419deca53e75907c27e5_a5ee1e2f6ae27419deca53e75907c27e5}{QCustom\+Plot\+::set\+Interactions} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a42cfbfd3052682539ed239795ae1c4a8_a42cfbfd3052682539ed239795ae1c4a8}\index{QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}!setSelectedParts@{setSelectedParts}}
\index{setSelectedParts@{setSelectedParts}!QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setSelectedParts()}{setSelectedParts()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a42cfbfd3052682539ed239795ae1c4a8_a42cfbfd3052682539ed239795ae1c4a8} 
void QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular\+::set\+Selected\+Parts (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular\+::\+Selectable\+Parts \&}]{selected\+Parts}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets the selected state of the respective axis parts described by \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a342afffd77fa1e8b30778b29a26eb416_a342afffd77fa1e8b30778b29a26eb416}{Selectable\+Part}. When a part is selected, it uses a different pen/font.

The entire selection mechanism for axes is handled automatically when \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot_a5ee1e2f6ae27419deca53e75907c27e5_a5ee1e2f6ae27419deca53e75907c27e5}{QCustom\+Plot\+::set\+Interactions} contains i\+Select\+Axes. You only need to call this function when you wish to change the selection state manually.

This function can change the selection state of a part, independent of the \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_af475366740d070e622e291dd30e26026_af475366740d070e622e291dd30e26026}{set\+Selectable\+Parts} setting.

emits the \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_aa20dfb49bdfae700a08c9280ccb0d2c9_aa20dfb49bdfae700a08c9280ccb0d2c9}{selection\+Changed} signal when {\itshape selected} is different from the previous selection state.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a361666cdcc6fbfd37344cc44be746b0f_a361666cdcc6fbfd37344cc44be746b0f} 
void QCPLayout\+Element\+::set\+Size\+Constraint\+Rect (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a0afb3e5773529e4bd20e448f81be4d2a_a0afb3e5773529e4bd20e448f81be4d2a}{Size\+Constraint\+Rect}}}]{constraint\+Rect}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Sets to which rect of a layout element the size constraints apply. Size constraints can be set via \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b}{set\+Minimum\+Size} and \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a74eb5280a737ab44833d506db65efd95_a74eb5280a737ab44833d506db65efd95}{set\+Maximum\+Size}.

The outer rect (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c}{outer\+Rect}) includes the margins (e.\+g. in the case of a \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect}{QCPAxis\+Rect} the axis labels), whereas the inner rect (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4}{rect}) does not.

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a460a6035eef606e5e23df175cd3eef08_a460a6035eef606e5e23df175cd3eef08}\index{QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}!setSubTickLength@{setSubTickLength}}
\index{setSubTickLength@{setSubTickLength}!QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setSubTickLength()}{setSubTickLength()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a460a6035eef606e5e23df175cd3eef08_a460a6035eef606e5e23df175cd3eef08} 
void QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular\+::set\+Sub\+Tick\+Length (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{inside}{, }\item[{int}]{outside}{ = {\ttfamily 0}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets the length of the subticks in pixels. {\itshape inside} is the length the subticks will reach inside the plot and {\itshape outside} is the length they will reach outside the plot. If {\itshape outside} is greater than zero, the tick labels and axis label will increase their distance to the axis accordingly, so they won\textquotesingle{}t collide with the ticks.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a4961b3541814e331c4cc29f66e709a45_a4961b3541814e331c4cc29f66e709a45} 
void QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular\+::set\+Sub\+Ticks (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{show}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets whether sub tick marks are displayed.

Sub ticks are only potentially visible if (major) ticks are also visible (see \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_ad2e017970a91fd11a7d19bed81e2be59_ad2e017970a91fd11a7d19bed81e2be59}{set\+Ticks})

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_ad2e017970a91fd11a7d19bed81e2be59_ad2e017970a91fd11a7d19bed81e2be59}{set\+Ticks} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a343fafde7e44cf32b7d89e45c9154bc8_a343fafde7e44cf32b7d89e45c9154bc8}\index{QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}!setTicker@{setTicker}}
\index{setTicker@{setTicker}!QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setTicker()}{setTicker()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a343fafde7e44cf32b7d89e45c9154bc8_a343fafde7e44cf32b7d89e45c9154bc8} 
void QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular\+::set\+Ticker (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{QShared\+Pointer$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_axis_ticker}{QCPAxis\+Ticker}} $>$}]{ticker}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

The axis ticker is responsible for generating the tick positions and tick labels. See the documentation of \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_ticker}{QCPAxis\+Ticker} for details on how to work with axis tickers.

You can change the tick positioning/labeling behaviour of this axis by setting a different \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_ticker}{QCPAxis\+Ticker} subclass using this method. If you only wish to modify the currently installed axis ticker, access it via \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a318206c22b5097ba6bb0f538200f345e_a318206c22b5097ba6bb0f538200f345e}{ticker}.

Since the ticker is stored in the axis as a shared pointer, multiple axes may share the same axis ticker simply by passing the same shared pointer to multiple axes.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a318206c22b5097ba6bb0f538200f345e_a318206c22b5097ba6bb0f538200f345e}{ticker} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\end{center}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_af0922fd33a9589524f1600f316ea673c_af0922fd33a9589524f1600f316ea673c} 
void QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular\+::set\+Tick\+Label\+Rotation (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{double}]{degrees}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets the rotation of the tick labels. If {\itshape degrees} is zero, the labels are drawn normally. Else, the tick labels are drawn rotated by {\itshape degrees} clockwise. The specified angle is bound to values from -\/90 to 90 degrees.

If {\itshape degrees} is exactly -\/90, 0 or 90, the tick labels are centered on the tick coordinate. For other angles, the label is drawn with an offset such that it seems to point toward or away from the tick mark. Here is the call graph for this function\+:\nopagebreak
\begin{figure}[H]
\begin{center}
\leavevmode
\includegraphics[width=350pt]{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_af0922fd33a9589524f1600f316ea673c_af0922fd33a9589524f1600f316ea673c_cgraph}
\end{center}
\end{figure}

\begin{center}

\end{center}
\end{figure}

void QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular\+::set\+Tick\+Labels (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{show}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets whether tick labels are displayed. Tick labels are the numbers drawn next to tick marks. \Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a3ac0147527231f74bc8a3c6311ad9d15_a3ac0147527231f74bc8a3c6311ad9d15}\index{QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}!setTickLength@{setTickLength}}
\index{setTickLength@{setTickLength}!QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setTickLength()}{setTickLength()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a3ac0147527231f74bc8a3c6311ad9d15_a3ac0147527231f74bc8a3c6311ad9d15} 
void QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular\+::set\+Tick\+Length (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{inside}{, }\item[{int}]{outside}{ = {\ttfamily 0}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets the length of the ticks in pixels. {\itshape inside} is the length the ticks will reach inside the plot and {\itshape outside} is the length they will reach outside the plot. If {\itshape outside} is greater than zero, the tick labels and axis label will increase their distance to the axis accordingly, so they won\textquotesingle{}t collide with the ticks.

Returns the top right corner of this axis rect in pixels. Margins are not taken into account here, so the returned value is with respect to the inner \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4}{rect}. \Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a9f2dfb377cdf3ce22a451fa9d3ab47e6_a9f2dfb377cdf3ce22a451fa9d3ab47e6}\index{QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}!update@{update}}
\index{update@{update}!QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{update()}{update()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a9f2dfb377cdf3ce22a451fa9d3ab47e6_a9f2dfb377cdf3ce22a451fa9d3ab47e6} 
void QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular\+::update (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a0d83360e05735735aaf6d7983c56374d_a0d83360e05735735aaf6d7983c56374d}{Update\+Phase}}}]{phase}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

This method is called automatically upon replot and doesn\textquotesingle{}t need to be called by users of \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular}{QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular}.

Calls the base class implementation to update the margins (see \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a929c2ec62e0e0e1d8418eaa802e2af9b_a929c2ec62e0e0e1d8418eaa802e2af9b}{QCPLayout\+Element\+::update}), and finally passes the \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4}{rect} to the inset layout (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_aab81c173315a73725150010a1893a17d_aab81c173315a73725150010a1893a17d}{inset\+Layout}) and calls its QCPInset\+Layout\+::update function.

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a78f5d8c2c942fa1c47dcef5d96616e8d_a78f5d8c2c942fa1c47dcef5d96616e8d}\index{QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}!wheelEvent@{wheelEvent}}
\index{wheelEvent@{wheelEvent}!QCPPolarAxisAngular@{QCPPolarAxisAngular}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{wheelEvent()}{wheelEvent()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_a78f5d8c2c942fa1c47dcef5d96616e8d_a78f5d8c2c942fa1c47dcef5d96616e8d} 
void QCPPolar\+Axis\+Angular\+::wheel\+Event (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{QWheel\+Event \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{event}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}

This event gets called when the user turns the mouse scroll wheel while the cursor is over the layerable. Whether a cursor is over the layerable is decided by a preceding call to \doxylink{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_abb390ae7656b7241acfe4ed9ea56f1ae_abb390ae7656b7241acfe4ed9ea56f1ae}{select\+Test}.

The current pixel position of the cursor on the \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot}{QCustom\+Plot} widget is accessible via {\ttfamily event-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}pos()}.

The {\ttfamily event-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}angle\+Delta()} indicates how far the mouse wheel was turned, which is usually +/-\/ 120 for single rotation steps. However, if the mouse wheel is turned rapidly, multiple steps may accumulate to one event, making the delta larger. On the other hand, if the wheel has very smooth steps or none at all, the delta may be smaller.

The default implementation does nothing.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_polar_axis_angular_abde756ec197666d7ee91eee11bc7c6d5_abde756ec197666d7ee91eee11bc7c6d5}
